/kloʊs/ adv.   (closer , clos·est) near; not far away 接近；靠近；紧挨着；不远地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They sat close together.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: fast. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">漩涡是由不断快速旋转的水形成的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Tuesday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">You consider me the young apprentice</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">你将我视为年轻学徒</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">Caugh</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> between the Scylla and Charybdis</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">使我进退两难</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> (The Police</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">乐队的歌曲</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">“Wrapped Around Your Finger”)</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">The</span></strong><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> online resource Encyclopedia Britannica explains tha</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> in Greek mythology, Scylla and Charybdis were two immortal monsters.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">网页版《大英百科全书》解释说，在希腊神话中，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">锡拉</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">和</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">卡律布狄斯</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">是两个不朽的怪物。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">They terrorized ships tha</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> tri</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">ed </span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">to travel the Strait of Messina, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a</strong> narrow waterway between Sicily and <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the</strong> Italian mainland.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">他们恐吓试图穿越墨西拿海峡的船只，墨西拿海峡是西西里岛和意大利大陆之间的狭窄水道。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">Scylla is the personification -- the human representation o</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">f a</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> non-human thing -- of sharp rocks and other objects along the coast. Scylla destroy</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">ed</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> ships tha</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> came too close.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">锡拉是海岸边锋利的岩石和其他物体的人格化</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">用人类来代表非人类的东西。</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">锡拉</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">摧毁靠太近的船只。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">Charybdis is the personification o</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">f a</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> whirlpool, a dangerous water formation in seas and oceans.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">卡律布狄斯是漩涡的化身，漩涡是海洋中的水形成的一种危险的形态。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">Charybdis also destroy</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">ed</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> ships tha</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> came too close but i</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;"> very different way.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;box-sizing: border-box;">卡律布狄斯也在以一种非常不同的（特有的）方式摧毁靠太近的船只。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The horse shied, just as it might have shied in the old, miserable days when it pulled a hansom. Then it roared. It strained its neck back as if there were a fly biting its shoulders and it wanted to scratch them. And then, just as the beasts had burst out of the earth, there burst out from the shoulders of Fledge wings that spread and grew, larger than eagles', larger than swans', larger than angels' wings in church windows. The feathers shone chestnut colour and copper colour. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那匹马吃惊地倒退了一步，在它拉车的悲惨岁月里，它可能也像今天这样受过惊。然后，它用后腿站起来，扭着脖子，仿佛想捉住叮咬它肩膀的苍蝇似的。接着，犹如动物们先前从地里蹦出来一样，弗兰奇的肩上钻出一对翅膀，越长越宽，越长越大，超过了鹰的翅膀、天鹅的翅膀和教堂窗户上天使的翅膀。这对翅膀的羽毛呈栗色和铜色。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A:我所有的时间都用来照顾孩子了，我感到累极了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B:为什么不要你丈夫帮你?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A:我试过了，但他拒绝帮我。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I spend all my time looking after my baby. I'm so tired.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Why don't you ask your husband to help you with it?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I've tried it, but he would have none of it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He is going to turn over a new leaf and work hard.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他将___________，努力工作。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">洗心革面</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">国务院办公厅日前印发通知，要求切实做好长江流域禁捕有关工作以及退捕渔民安置保障工作。通知提出，长江流域禁捕是保护长江和加强生态文明建设的重要举措，沿江各地政府和各有关部门要细化完善各项政策措施，全面抓好落实。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">China called for solid efforts to implement the fishing ban in the Yangtze River basin, and ensure the livelihoods of affected fishermen after they bid farewell to nets and boats, according to a circular released by the General Office of the State Council. As the fishing ban in the Yangtze River basin is an important measure to protect the river and improve the ecological environment, local governments and related departments should roll out specific policies and measures to ensure its implementation, the circular said.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;'><strong style="outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;">10.19 每日一句：</strong><strong><span lang="EN-US" style='font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;text-align: justify;'>I don't know what to say.</span></strong></p><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;'><strong><span lang="EN-US" style='font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;text-align: justify;'>我不知说什么好。</span></strong></p><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">2163</span></span></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(166, 91, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>用法有三：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→fear to do XX 害怕/畏惧做...</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">feared to</span></em></strong> tell him the truth. </p><p style="white-space: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My son <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">to</span></em></strong> touch a dog. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我儿子<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">害怕</strong>摸狗。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">fear to</span></em></strong> go into those mines.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你<strong style="box-sizing: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: dying. 勇敢的士兵不<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">怕</strong>死。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">=Brave soldiers do not <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">fear </span></em></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: soldiers do not <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">fear</span></em></strong> death.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>In the cave you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">fear to</span></em></strong> enter lies the treasure you seek.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在你<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">不敢</strong>踏足的洞穴里，蕴藏着你在寻找的宝藏。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">fear to</span></em></strong> find out what the answer is.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">害怕</strong>找出答案。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">   活学活用</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);padding: 0px 9px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请用<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">fear to do XX/ fear doing XX/ fear XX</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong>随意造句</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1. vice versa </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">反之亦然，是一个外来词组，来自与拉丁文。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">E.g : Men should respect women or vice versa. 男人应该尊重女人，反过来一样。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This occurs when the left ear hears some of the sound coming from the right speaker, and vice versa. 发生这现象是因为从右侧喇叭发出的声音，左耳会听到一部分，反之亦然。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">or vice versa 和 and vice versa的区别</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A and B 指的是AB</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A or B 指的是A或B</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所以and vice versa 指的是双项，or vice versa更多指的是单项</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. 【Idiom】</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the lesser of two evils：the less unpleasant of two choices, neither of which is good两害相权取其轻，最初仅用来指道德上的选择，但现在当需要在两件不好的事情、两个不好的人或两种不好的情况中作一选择，都可以使用了。两种罪恶中，选择罪恶较小的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">evil  /ˈiːvəl/ noun.  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">something that is very bad and harmful邪恶（之事）；罪恶（行为）；祸害；灾祸</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">         adj.morally bad, cruel, or very unpleasant道德败坏的；邪恶的，恶毒的；讨厌的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. dilemma </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/dəˈlemə, daɪˈlemə, dɪˈlemə/ noun </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a situation in which a difficult choice has to be made between two different things you could do左右为难，两难境地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">COLLOCATIONS:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be in a dilemma 进退两难   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">face a dilemma/be faced with a dilemma面临困境、面对困境</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Women may still be faced with the dilemma of choosing between jobs and families.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">女性可能仍然面临着在工作和家庭之间做出选择的困境。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">pose/create a dilemma 构成/制造困境</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">put/place somebody in a dilemma 将某人置于两难境地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">resolve/solve a dilemma 解决困境</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">explain your dilemma 解释你的困境（=谈论它）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. pickle </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈpɪkəl/ noun </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vegetables or fruit that have been preserved in a vinegar sauce or salty water腌菜，泡菜；菜酱，醋渍黄瓜（片）；腌黄瓜（片）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(be) In a pickle，处于困境，左右两难。“in a pickle”不是指“在泡菜里”</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">进退两难的意思是指前进和后退都难。比喻事情无法决定，因而难以行动，处境困难。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">近义词：进退维亟、进退维谷、骑虎难下、势成骑虎、左右为难、进退迍（zhūn）邅（zhān）、跋（bá）前疐（zhì）后：《诗经·豳风·狼跋》：“狼跋其胡，载疐其尾。” 意思是说狼向前进就踩着它的胡（下巴下面下垂的肉），往后退就被尾巴绊倒。后用“跋前疐后”比喻进退两难。疐（zhì）：跌倒。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“进退两难”英文表述如下：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">between a rock and a hard place</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">on the horns of a dilemma</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">between the devil and the deep blue sea</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">between Scylla and Charybdis</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“进退两难”中文近义词如下：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">进退维亟、进退维谷</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">骑虎难下</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">势成骑虎</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">左右为难</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">进退迍（zhūn）邅（zhān）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">跋（bá）前疐（zhì）后</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">腹背受敌</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px;padding-left: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读 <span style="font-size: 14px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Wednesday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> both coul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> kill you! And they were located so close to each other tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> they gave sailors an almost impossible choice.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">但两者都有可能杀死你！他们相距很近，让水手们别无他选。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Avoiding Charybdis meant passing too close to Scylla and vice versa.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">避开卡律布狄斯就意味着会离锡拉很近，反之亦然。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">An<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> is wha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> "being betwee<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span> rock and har<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> place" means.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这就是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">“being between a rock and hard place(</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">进退两难</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">)”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">的意思，</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">You are in a<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n i</span></span>mpossibly difficul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> sit<span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">u<sup style="box-sizing: border-box;">(w)</sup>a</span>tion with no good choices.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">就是说</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">“</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你正处在一个难以想象的困境中，没有好的选择。</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">”</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">So really, you must choose between the lesser of two evils.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">所以，你必须在两害相权取其轻。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Now, let's hear this used i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span> conversation between two friends.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">现在，我们来听听这个短语在两个朋友之间的对话中的用法。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">A woman is planni<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ng a</span></span> birthday party for her son.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">一位女士正在为她的儿子筹划一场生日聚会。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">An<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span> friend who offers to help finds himself in a dilemma, a real pickle – you know a difficult situation!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">而一个主动提供帮助的朋友却发现自己陷入了一个困境，一个真正的困境</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你知道的，一个困难的处境！</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">He has a har<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> decision to make.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">他有一个艰难的决定要做。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Can I help with the birthday party?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我能帮忙办生日派对吗？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Oh yes! Thank you so much!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">哦，可以！非常感谢！</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Of course! It's your son's birthday. I'm happy to help.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">嗯呐！今天是你儿子的生日，我很乐意帮忙。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">All Narnia, many-coloured with lawns and rocks and heather and different sorts of trees, lay spread out below them, the river winding through it like a ribbon of quicksilver. They could already see over the tops of the low hills which lay northward on their right; beyond those hills a great moorland sloped gently up and up to the horizon. On their left the mountains were much higher, but every now and then there was a gap when you could see, between steep pine woods, a glimpse of the southern lands that lay beyond them, looking blue and far away.   </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">整个纳尼亚展开在他们脚下，草地、岩石、石南属植物和千姿百态的树木将大地染得五彩缤纷，蜿蜒的河流像一条水银的带子。右望北方，小山的那一边，是一片缓缓斜升至地平线的沼地。左边的山高得多，但不时可见一个个峡谷。从那儿望过去，透过挺拔的松林，能瞥见南方蔚蓝的土地，远远地绵延伸展。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A:什么是生活?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B:别问这样的问题，没有固定的答案，每个人在内心里都会有个答案。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A:那你说人生是不是由什么高于我们的东西安排的?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B:或许吧，命运的变迁，谁知道?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A:就是。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: What is life?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Don't ask such a question. You know it has no certain answer. Everyone knows it in his heart.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Then do you think that life is arranged by something abouve us?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Maybe, the whirligig of time, who knows?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Right.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Would you please give your withdrawal slip and your passbook?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请把您的取款条和_________给我好吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">存折</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">目前，教育在我们国家总支出中仅占4%。相比之下，一些发达国家在教育方面的支出达10%左右。政府在学前教育方面的资金投入严重缺乏，今后亟待改善。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Education now only accounts for 4 percent of the country's total expenditures. By comparison, the figure in some developed countries is around 10 percent. We also have a sore lack of government investment in preschool education, which should be enhanced in the future.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box 每日一句：</strong><strong><span lang="EN-US" style='font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;text-align: justify;'>You promised me.   </span></strong></p><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">10.21 早读原文</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: 0px;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: 0.2em;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.44);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.44);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">It's foolish to run the risk of going mad for vanity's sake.</span></strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>1. foolish /uː/  区分 full/ʊ/</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>2. vanity's sake  vanity's尾音/z/，sake首音/s/ → 后进同化</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：it's foolish to do XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">foolish adj. 愚蠢的；傻的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">近义词：stupid/silly</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It was <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">foolish</span></strong></em> of them to pay so much.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们花了这么多钱，真<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">傻</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It would be <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">foolish</span></em></strong> to change your mind now. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在改变主意太<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">愚蠢</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：run the risk (of sth/of doing XX) / run risks</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">冒…的危险；冒险做某事</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We don't want to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">run the risk of</span></em></strong> losing their business.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们不想<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">冒险</strong>失去他们的生意。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>They might <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">run the risk of</span></em></strong> becoming obsolete.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">它们可能会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">面临</strong>被淘汰的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">风险</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>We <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">run the risk of</span></em></strong> making the same mistake again.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">冒着</strong>再次犯同样错误的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">风险</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> Your men will <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">run the risk of </span></em></strong>being spotted.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你的人很可能被发现。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So, you <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">run the risk of</span></em></strong> looking like you're covering it up, and that's a hell of a risk.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你处理起来就像隐瞒事实，这风险很大。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6268519" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《太空堡垒卡拉狄加》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. 词链儿：go mad</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→go mad (=become very angry) 生气，发火</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Look at this mess! Mum will <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">go mad</span></em></strong>!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">瞧这一团糟！妈妈会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">很生气的</strong>！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→go </strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">mad  发疯的</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">、神经错乱的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I’d <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">go mad</span></em></strong> (=start to feel crazy) if I was stuck at home all day.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果我整天困在家里我会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">发疯的</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">拓展词链儿：do</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">n’t</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> go mad</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">别不要命地干；别太激动；别乱花钱</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I know you’ve got a lot to do but <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">don’t go mad</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我知道你有许多事情要做，但也<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">别太拼命</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">‘I'm going to buy some new clothes.’</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">‘Well, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">don't go mad</span></em></strong> (= spend more than is sensible).’</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“我要去买几件新衣服。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“去吧，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">可别乱花钱</strong>。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-linktype="2" href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653542301&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=01d5f28f6bfcaba7574be2b021d01ee8&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="点击链接跳转回顾【go mad 近义表达】">点击链接跳转回顾【go mad 近义表达】</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">4. 词链儿：for XX's sake</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">为XX本身的缘故；鉴于XX本身的价值</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">art <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">for art's sake</span></em></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">为艺术</strong>而艺术</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Do it <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">for my sake</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">为了我的缘故</strong>，你就做这件事吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">For safety's sake</span></em></strong>, never stand directly behind a horse.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">为安全起见</strong>，千万别站在马的正后方。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-linktype="2" href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653537261&amp;idx=2&amp;sn=f92eda13e1d4b57e53f191bcf36f7c0b&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="点击链接跳转回顾 【for old times' sake】">点击链接跳转回顾 【for old times' sake】</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: border-box;">for your sake</span></em></strong>, for the sake of Harper.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你必须放开我，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">为了你</strong>，也为了哈勃。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">虽然我得和一群<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">土气主妇</span>一起购物，但不代表我就得打扮得像她们一样。</p><p style="text-align: left;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display:
