</section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vet</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/vet/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 诊疗；审查 vi. 作兽医；诊疗 n. 兽医</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Go to the vet if unsure.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">不确定的话记得去咨询兽医。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Voters took their job of vetting the candidates seriously.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">选民们认真对待他们审查候选人的工作。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">promise </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈprɒmɪs ; ˈprɑːmɪs/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 许诺，允诺；希望</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 允诺，许诺；给人以…的指望或希望</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 许诺；有指望，有前途</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A promise is a promise, " Hermione reminded Harry bossily.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“一言既出，驷马难追。”赫敏盛气凌人地提醒哈利。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The day dawned bright and clear, with the promise of warm, sunny weather. 拂晓时晴空万里，预示着温暖晴朗的天气。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ice cream 冰淇淋</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Desserts are served with cream or ice cream. 甜点上加奶油或冰淇淋。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We've got chocolate ice cream, vanilla ice cream and rainbow sherbet.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们有巧克力冰激凌、香草冰激凌和彩虹刨冰。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">either </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈaɪðə(r)  ;  ˈiːðə(r)  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">pron. (两者之中)任何一个</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. (两者中)任一的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adv. (否定句中)也</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 非此即彼的, 两者择一的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So for about 25 years, the painting was either unviewed and was either in storage.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">近25年来，这幅画要么无人问津，要么作为储藏品。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Either pronunciation and spelling can be used for either one, depending on who's talking.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">任意一种发音和拼写都可以使用，取决于谁在说话。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">probably </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈprɒbəbli  ;  ˈprɑːbəbli  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adv. 大概; 或许; 可能</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> It was the best known and probably the most popular of her songs. 这是她最著名的、大概也是她最受欢迎的歌曲。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ready for a nap 准备小睡一会儿</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ready for 对...有准备</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">get ready for 为……做准备</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We were getting ready for Tommy's party.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们在为汤米的派对做准备。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">nap</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/næp/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 小睡，打盹儿；细毛；孤注一掷</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 使拉毛 vi. 小睡；疏忽</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Nap time is about to end.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">午休时间快结束了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">tired</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/'taɪəd/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 疲倦的；厌倦的，厌烦的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v. 疲倦；对…腻烦（tire的过去分词形式）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I am somewhat tired of this work.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我对这个工作有点厌倦了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Why? Tired of walking in those heels?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">咋了 厌倦了穿高跟鞋走远路吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">quiet </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈkwaɪət/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> making very little noise 轻声的；轻柔的；安静的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She crept downstairs (as) quiet as a mouse. 她蹑手蹑脚，悄声下了楼</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">irritable </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈɪrɪtəbl/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 易怒的, 急躁的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adv. irritably</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But Tom, full of years and irritable at disturbances, switched his tail and spat softly.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">谁知汤姆上了几岁年纪，不喜欢打扰，竖起尾巴，发出了低沉的吼叫声。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">" I'm an irritable wallflower who's dangerously curious."</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">" 我是一个容易发怒又不善交际的人，好奇心强得厉害。"</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">over-excited </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">过度兴奋的；兴奋得忘乎所以的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> Don't get the children overexcited just before bedtime. 临睡前不要让孩子玩得过于兴奋。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">sugar </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈʃʊɡə(r)/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 糖；食糖；甜言蜜语</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 加糖于；粉饰 vi. 形成糖</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We were primarily a sugar plantation town.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们镇基本上就是个糖料种植场。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">After all, we use sugar for energy.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">毕竟，我们靠糖来获得能量。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">but then again 话说回来</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's a long title, but then again, it's a long book.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">书名很长，但话说回来，这本书的故事也很长。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a dog person 喜欢狗的人，狗控</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And as for Herculano-Houzel herself, she is 100 percent a dog person.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">至于苏珊娜本人，她可是个十足的“狗控”呢。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So, you would say you're definitely a cat person and not a dog person?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那你是爱猫人士，而不是爱狗人士吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">hate </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ heɪt / vt. </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">憎恨, 讨厌,不愿, 不喜欢,为…感到抱歉 n. 憎恨; 厌恶,所恨的人或物</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Love, hate, joy, and fear are emotions.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">爱、恨、喜、惧都是情感。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Love and hate are extremes of passion.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">爱与恨是感情的两个极端。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">bark</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/bɑ:k/ vi. 吠叫 vt. 大声喊出</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 犬吠声, 狐狸的嗥叫声,树皮。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He barked questions at her. 他厉声质问她。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">whole </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ həʊl  ; hoʊl/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We drank a whole bottle each. 我们每人都喝了整整一瓶。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It inspired a whole generation of musicians.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专辑激发了整整一代音乐家。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">overly</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/'əʊvəli/ adv.过度地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He doesn't need to use overly complex vocabulary.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他不需要使用太复杂的词汇。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">messy </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈmesi / adj. 肮脏的，污秽的；凌乱的，散乱的；麻烦的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I can't find anything on this messy desk.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">在这张堆放得乱七八糟的桌子上我什么也找不到。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The divorce was painful and messy. 那次离婚令人痛苦而又纠葛不清。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">pay </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ peɪ v/vt. 支付，付；偿还，补偿</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 付款；偿还 n. 工资，薪水；付款</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> May I pay by credit card?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我可以用信用卡付款吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So they are paid for work. They are not paid for not working.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">工作就有钱拿，请假就不发工资。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">afterward </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/'ɑːftəwəd; 'æftərwəd/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adv. 以后, 过后, 后来</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Why do people feel sort of crummy afterward?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">为什么人们注射后会感到不适？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So afterward everything is just kind of wiped out.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">那之后一切都会被摧毁。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">choose </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ tʃuːz /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 选择，决定 vi. 选择，挑选</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This site has been chosen for the new school. 这块场地已被选作新学校的校址。And you have to choose two. You can't choose all three.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你只能选择其中两个。不能三个都选。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Well, I nee<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> to take my dog to the vet later today. Bu<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t I </span></span>also promised my son tha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t I</span></span> woul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d </span></span>take him and his friends out for ice cream after the party. So, can you either take the dog or the kids?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">今天晚些时候我要带我的狗去看兽医。但是我还答应了儿子晚会结束后带他和他的朋友们出去吃冰淇淋。能麻烦你带狗去看兽医或者带孩子去吃冰淇淋吗？</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Ah ... how many kids?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">啊</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">……</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">有多少孩子？</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Seven. No wai<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span>. Eight. And they will probably all be ready for a nap.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">7</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">个，等下，是</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">8</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">个，他们大概都准备好小睡了。</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">  </span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">So they'll be tire<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span>n<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> quiet?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">所以他们会很累很安静吗？</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">No. They will be irritable and over-excited because they've ha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> too much sugar.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">不，他们会变得急躁和兴奋，因为他们吃了太多的糖。</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Argh. Tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span>sounds terrible. Bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> the<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span>gain, I'm no<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> really a dog person. Is she goo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d i</span></span>n the car?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">啊，听起来很糟糕。但话说回来，我也不太喜欢狗，她待在车里乖吗？</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">She ha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">tes i</span></span>t! Bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> no<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span>s mu<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">ch a</span></span>s she hates the doctor. She will probably bark the whole time.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">她不喜欢待在车里，但她更讨厌医生，她可能会一直叫。</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Okay. So, I can either ta<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">ke a</span></span>n unhappy, barking dog to the vet. Or I can ta<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">ke a</span></span> car fu<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">ll o</span></span>f overly excite<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> six-year-olds out for messy ice cream.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">好吧。所以说就是，我要不带一只不开心的狗去看兽医，要不带一车兴奋过度的</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">6</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">岁小孩出去吃乱七八糟的冰淇淋。</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Right. Bu<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t I</span></span>'ll pay for the ice cream and I'll pay to have your car cleaned afterward – no matter which one you choose.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">是的。不过我会付你买冰淇淋的钱，或者付你洗车的钱</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">不管你选哪一个。</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Well?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">嗯？</span></p><p style="text-indent: 32px;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">For now a great barrier of cliffs rose before them and they were almost dazzled by the sunlight dancing on the great waterfall by which the river roars and sparkles down into Narnia itself from the high western lands in which it rises. They were flying so high already that the thunder of those falls could only just be heard as a small, thin sound, but they were not yet high enough to fly over the top of the cliffs.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">悬崖峭壁在他们眼前竖起一道巨大的屏障，阳光在大瀑布上闪烁，令人目眩。来自西边高地的河水咆哮着，水花飞溅地流进纳尼亚境内。他们已经飞得很高，瀑布雷鸣般的巨响已变得很轻。但他们飞行的高度还不能越过峭壁。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A:我大姨怀孕了，老想吐。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：她应该多喝开水，多休息。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A:但她觉得整天待在家里一点胃口也没有。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：别担心，她很快就会好起来的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: My elder aunt feels like vomiting, she is pregnant.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: She'd better drink plenty of hot water and lie in bed.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: But she feels like having no appetite at all if she stays at home all day.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Don't worry. She'll be all right.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A good negotiator always has more than one ace in the hole.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">谈判高手总有数张_________在手。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">王牌</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中国每年有成千上万名学生出国留学。但是，主要的留学国家大都是欧美发达国家。“一带一路”沿线经过了许多亚洲、非洲以及拉丁美洲等地的欠发达国家，但中国学生对这些国家的历史、社会、文化和宗教信仰状况都缺乏了解。需要大力培养对“一带一路”沿线国家有充分认识的人才，为中国投资者迈向世界助一臂之力。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">There are thousands of Chinese students studying abroad every year. However, the majority of destinations are developed countries in Europe and the United States. They know little about the history, society, culture and religious situations of the less-developed countries along the routes of the Belt and Road in Asia, Africa and Latin America. The amount of talent with a good understanding of countries along the routes needs to increase for Chinese investors to go global.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica border-box;">1. 我交了好运。</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 让他听由天命</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>1. call</strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>s u</strong></span><strong>po</strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>n u</strong></span><strong>s / a</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);text-decoration: underline;"><strong>t a</strong></span><strong> momen</strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>t of our</strong></span><strong>  词间连贯；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>2. choosing /tʃuː/不要发“出”，注意/tʃ/到/uː/的过渡。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> 1. fate &amp; destiny &amp; fortune 词汇辨析</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ destiny:</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">普通用词，侧重预先注定的命运，对未来命运的美好憧憬。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Something was about to happen that would shape her <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">destiny</span></strong></em>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">决定她<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">命运</strong>的事情即将发生。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-linktype="2" href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653549254&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=34639050e9306db52f20d51711110132&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="点击链接跳转 XX is one's true destiny">点击链接跳转 XX is one's true destiny</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→fate:</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">较庄严用词，多指不幸的命运，暗示不可避免，令人畏惧和人的意志无法改变，宿命论色彩较浓。 </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They had abandoned him and <span style="text-decoration: underline;">left him to his <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">fate</span></em></strong></span> .</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们把他丢下不管，让他听天由<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">命</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→fortune:</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">普通用词，（尤指影响人生的）机会；由机会或运气来决定的一种命运，如暗示一种比fate好的运气或一种愉快的未来。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Fortune</span></em></strong> smiled on me (= I had good luck). </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我交了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">好运</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：call on/upon XX 呼吁，号召</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I now <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">call upon</span></em></strong> the chairman to address the meeting.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请</strong>主席向大会致辞。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"> ★原声例句：</span></strong>There is no other name for men to<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"> call upon</span></em></strong> to save them.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">人们没有其他的名字可以<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">召唤</strong>来拯救他们。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"> ★原声例句：</span></strong>And every time I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">call upon</span></em></strong> it, I am awakened.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">每当我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">呼唤</strong>它时，我就会被唤醒。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">call upon</span></em></strong> you in this, our hour of need.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们在需要的时候<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">呼唤</strong>你。</p></section><section style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Food supplies <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">run low</strong> after natural disasters happened.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">自然灾害后，食物供给<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">跟不上</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 20px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(116, 111, 143);letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.8;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;padding: 0px 23px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">📃Past the worst, most difficult, or most stressful part (of something)</em><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">渡过最不好、最艰难、最有压力的阶段</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"></em></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;width: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">✅例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I know we have tried over and over again, but we're finally <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">over the hump</strong>. Everything should go smoothly now.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我知道我们已经反复尝试了，但是我们最终还是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">克服了困难</strong>。目前一切进展顺利。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'll be <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">over the hump</strong> when I've done this exam— then there'll be just two left.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">考完这门我就<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">轻松</strong>了，只剩下两门了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">相比“能够坚持下去，渡过难关”，那么“做到一半”怎么讲？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">halfway done (with something)</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">做（进行）到一半</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's quite challenging but we are almost<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> halfway done</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所以，这还是比较困难的，但我们几乎<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">完成了一半</strong>。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">dilemma  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/dəˈlemə, daɪ-/ a situation in which it is very difficult to decide what to do, because all the choices seem equally good or equally bad n.（进退两难的）窘境</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Many women are faced with the dilemma of choosing between work and family commitments.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">weigh option 衡量；权衡</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Damned if you do, damned if you don't ：used to say that whatever you say or do will be considered wrong</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be angry at 对...气愤</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be (get) angry with sb. 生某人的气</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be angry about 对...感到气愤</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">*angry at sth.与angry about sth.的区别:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">angry at指在事情发生时很气愤;而angry about则指在事情发生后已一段时间仍很气愤。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Don't be angry with me for not having written.别因为我没有写信而生我的气。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The professor was angry at John for cheating in the exam.教授对约翰考试作弊十分气恼。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The old woman often gets angry about trivial things.老太太常因琐屑小事发火。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;padding: 3px 10px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: right;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">第三步   认真校对，查缺补漏</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 87);height: 1.2em;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style='border-radius: 100%;margin-left: -0.8em;display: inline-block;float: left;width: 1.6em;height: 1.6em;background-position: center 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span I ha</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ve a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> dilemma. I'm still weighing my options. They are both so bad!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">我不知道！我现在进退两难，我还在权衡我的选择，无论选哪个都不好！</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">I didn't mean to pu</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> you betwee</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> ro</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ck a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">nd har</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> place. Bu</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">you did offer.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">我不是有意让你进退两难的，但你确实说要帮我什么的</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">……</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">Now, you may have also heard the expression: Damne</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d i</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">f you do, damne</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d i</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">f you don't!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">你可能还听过这样的表达：</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">“Damned if you do, damned if you don't!”</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">This may sound the sa</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">me a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">s "being betwee</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> rock an</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> hard place" but we use it a little differently.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">听起来可能和</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">“being between a rock and a hard place(</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">处于两难境地</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">)”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">一样，但用法略有不同。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">If you are damne</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d i</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">f you do, damne</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d i</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">f you don't – i</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> means tha</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(79, 129, 189);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> no matter what you do, someone is going to b</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">ngry or upset with you.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">“If you are damned if you do, damned if you don't”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">意思就是无论你做什么，总会有人对你生气。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">Being between a rock an</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> hard place involves your choosing between two terrible choices.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">“be between a rock and a hard place”</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">说的是你要在两个可怕的选择中做出选择。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">Now whenever you have to choose between these expressions, you will know which one to use.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">现在，当你要在这些表达方式中做出选择时你就会知道该使用哪一个。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">And luckily choosing between them will not put you betwee</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> rock an</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;"> hard place.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;background: white;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(68, 68, 68);box-sizing: border-box;">幸运的是，在他们之间做出选择不会让你陷入两难境地。</span></p><p style="line-height: 19px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Now they were over the top of the cliffs and in a few minutes the valley land of Narnia had sunk out of sight behind them. They were flying over a wild country of steep hills and dark forests, still following the course of the river. The really big mountains loomed ahead. But the sun was now in the travelers’ eyes and they couldn't see things very clearly in that direction. For the sun sank lower and lower till the western sky was all like one great furnace full of melted gold; and it set at last behind a jagged peak which stood up against the brightness as sharp and flat as if it were cut out of cardboard.    </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们已经飞上了悬崖之巅，几分钟后，纳尼亚谷地就从后面的视野中消失了。他们沿着河流，飞行在一片蛮荒的土地上，下面是陡峭的山坡和黑魃魃的森林。前面隐隐出现雄伟的高山。阳光从正前方射来，使他们看不清前面的景物。这时，太阳正在落山，西边的天空像一个巨大的熔炉，装满了熔化的黄金。终于，夕阳沉匿在锯齿状的山峰背后，一片辉煌映衬着仿佛从纸片上剪下的、清晰而失去了立体感的群山。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：别太难过了，如果你真觉得和他一点感情都没有，那么，依我看，离婚或许是解决问题的最好方法。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：我心里很清楚，只不过放心不下孩子。她还小，不能了解我们，也无法接受这样的事实。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A：对呀，孩子是个问题，干脆别告诉珍妮实情，等她大了，找个合适的机会再告诉她。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B：我明白，就这样吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Don’t be too sad. If you really think that you have no feeling with him, then, in my opinion, getting divorced maybe is the best ways to solve the problem.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I know clearly at the bottom of my heart. I just can't set my mind at rest because of the child. She's little. She cannot understand us and accept such truth.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yeah, child is the matter. Don't tell Jenny the truth, only tell her the white lie. When she grows up, you find the suitable opportunity to tell her.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I see, OK.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We hope for a lasting settlement of all these troubles.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们希望这些纠纷能获得__________解决。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">永久的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">到今年，我做教育做了40年，集40年之经验，我可以非常负责任的跟大家说，家庭是孩子的第一所学校，父母是孩子的第一任老师。家庭教育在培养孩子的意识观念和适应能力上起着至关重要的作用。所以我建议家长把更多的时间花在家庭教育上，而不是花费时间和金钱选择最好的学校。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">As an educator with more than 40 years of experience, I believe that family is the first school for children. Parents are the first teachers for their children, and family education is vital in terms of cultivating children's minds and adaptability. I suggest parents should devote more time to family education instead of too much time and money in choosing the best schools.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style='text-align: center;outline: 0px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">can't no more 在歌词中的含义是？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A  不能没有更多   B  不再（比can't any more 语气更强）</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="3. Our doubts are traitors and make us lose the good we oft might win by fearing to attempt.</a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">lose、good 包含的元音分别是：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A /uː/ /ʊ/    B /uː/ /uː/   C /ʊ/ /uː/ </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653555957&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=eabcf9c83ee990a4b6bf43de09c2d231&amp;chksm=f7ebcc38c09c452e9e41104360e710f2808df0a89f8823de2e13de4936055a186dc66aa11503&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="4. border-box;"></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.0828125" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/sz_mmbiz_png/x5BIsQKGnRicxHXZswnEb2nCZfQucyeNoJcWPN9lsUWM8GhpC7rUzwvLdac2Xx3EaIA0EYpepbic2w7BYW3Sx02g/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="640" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">本文挖了几个空</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">试着填出来吧～</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You weren't there.你爽约了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You didn't come.你没来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I don't understand.我不明白。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Something must have happened. I'm sorry.一定是出事了，对不起。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I've got two years, Kate. We can try again.我有两年的时间我们可以再约。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">No, Alex, it's too late.不用了，来不及了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It already happened. It didn't work.事情已经发生，没有用的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Don't give up on me, Kate.别放弃。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What about Persuasion? You told me. They wait. 《劝导》是怎么写的？你告诉过我，他们等了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They meet again, they have another chance.于是重逢，又有另一次机会。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Life is not a book, Alex.人生不是小说。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And it can be over in a second.瞬间就可能结束。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I was having lunch with my mother at Daley Plaza and a man was killed right in front of me.我在戴利广场陪我妈吃午饭，有个人在我面前被车撞死。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He died in my arms.他死在我怀里。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And I thought: "It can't end just like that on valentine's Day. "我心想“不可能就那样在情人节当天结束。”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1_____________________________________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And then I thought: "What if there is no one?"于是我想“要是没人等他呢？”</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">What if you live your whole life and no one is waiting? 要是活了一辈子却没人在家里等你呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">So I drove to the lake house looking for any kind of answer.所以我开车到湖畔小屋找答案。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And I found you.我找到了你。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And I let myself get lost.我让自己迷失了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2__________________________________.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But it's not real, Alex.但那不够真实。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I have to learn to live the life that I have got.我要学会面对现有的生活。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Please don't write anymore.请你别再写信了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Don't try to find me.不要来找我。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Let me let you go.让我对你释怀。</p></section><section
